[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing run against the HTML parsing component triggered a critical [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity finding: an OS command injection vulnerability. The fuzzer’s input caused [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution of attacker-controlled data via Java’s ProcessBuilder/Runtime.exec APIs, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresulting in a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` alert. The crash originates from [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache Tika’s `ExternalParser.parse` method when invoked through the HTML parser [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis issue report describes an OS command injection vulnerability detected during [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz testing. Key observations:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is identified as “OS Command Injection,” where untrusted input is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed to operating system commands, posing a risk of arbitrary code execution.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Fuzzer alert and stack trace  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The Jazzer sanitizer for OS command injection [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`OsCommandInjection.processImplStartHook`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m flagged the execution of a command [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuilt from attacker-controlled data. The call stack shows transitions from the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer hook into `ProcessBuilder.start` and `Runtime.exec`, then into Apache [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika’s `ExternalParser.parse` routines.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Involved code paths  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Tika’s `ExternalParser.parse` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m274[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m314[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: constructs and executes [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal commands.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The HTML parsing pipeline [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`HtmlHandler`, `JSoupParser`, `AutoDetectParser`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39metc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that eventually delegates to `ExternalParser`.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Fuzzer harness methods [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`HtmlParserFuzzer.parseOne` and `fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mserve as the entry point but are not the root cause.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Points of investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To gain a holistic understanding, review:  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. ExternalParser implementation in Apache Tika, including how it builds [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand-line invocations.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Data flow from the HTML parser through `HtmlHandler` and `JSoupParser`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mespecially how URI schemes or embedded content trigger external parsing.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Any configuration or sanitization layers around `Runtime.exec` or [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ProcessBuilder` calls in Tika.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness only as an entry, confirming the location where untrusted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput crosses into OS command execution.[0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ExternalParser builds an OS command invocation by naively splitting or copying[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe user-provided `command` array, then calls `[0m[1;35mRuntime.exec[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m307[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In HTML parsing, untrusted HTML content can set the `html_met[0m[1;92ma:e[0m[39mxiftool_path` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata, which flows into `HtmlHandler.configureExifTool` and ultimately into [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mExternalParser.setCommand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath, [0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32mIN[0m[1;33mPUT[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Because both the binary path string [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`path`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the placeholder substitution [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare attacker-controlled—and because `ExternalParser` uses `Runtime.exec` with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msingle string or space-split string—the fuzzer can inject shell metacharacters or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchain unexpected commands, leading to OS command injection.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy Overview[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Tighten the configuration source for external parser commands  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Do **not** allow untrusted HTML metadata to dictate executable paths. Treat[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`html_met[0m[1;92ma:e[0m[39mxiftool_path` as content data only; any override of the exiftool binary[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath must come from Tika’s application configuration [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `TikaConfig.xml`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystem property, or ParserContext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Add stringent validation and whitelisting for any externally configured [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – For the exiftool path [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor any `ExternalParser` command[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, verify that:  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • It is an absolute or well-known installation path,  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • The file exists and is executable [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`File#[0m[1;35mexists[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && File#[0m[1;35mcanExecute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • It contains no whitespace or shell metacharacters [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`;`, `&`, `|`, `` ` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m``, `>`, `<`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Reject or log-and-skip any configuration that fails validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthrow a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TikaException` or skip external parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Replace `Runtime.exec` with `ProcessBuilder` and avoid ad-hoc splitting  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – In `[0m[1;35mExternalParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, remove the special-case logic that splits a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msingle command string by spaces. Instead:  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Store the command tokens exactly as configured [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia a `List<String>` or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidated `String[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Construct a `ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmdTokens[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Propagate environment modifications via `[0m[1;35mpb.environment[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` if needed.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Call `Process process = [0m[1;35mpb.start[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – This ensures that each token is passed as a literal argument, and that no [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshell interpolation occurs.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Preserve existing functionality  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Legitimate uses of exiftool and other external parsers still work if [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfigured correctly via Tika’s standard configuration mechanisms.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Existing tests and harness code remain unchanged; only the production [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ExternalParser` logic and the HTML module’s metadata-handling paths are patched.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Step-by-Step Patch Plan[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In HtmlHandler [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtika-parser-html-module[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Remove or disable usage of `[0m[1;35mmetadata.get[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"html_meta:exiftool_path"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` as a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msource for the exiftool binary.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m If an application truly needs to override the path, expose it via [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mParserContext or TikaConfig, **not** via HTML metadata.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In ExternalParser:  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Change the internal storage of commands to a `List<String> commandTokens`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpopulated via `[0m[1;35msetCommand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mList<String>[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Deprecate/override the existing `[0m[1;35msetCommand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString, String[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` so that it[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidates each token against a safe-character regex and filesystem checks.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Remove lines [0m[1;36m290[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m296[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35m.split[0m[1;39m([0m[32m" "[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m entirely; assume the caller has [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovided already‐tokenized, validated arguments.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Replace the `[0m[1;35mRuntime.getRuntime[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.exec[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m311[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m314[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with:  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```java[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommandTokens[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39menvironmentOverrides != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mpb.environment[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.putAll[0m[1;39m([0m[39menvironmentOverrides[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         Process process = [0m[1;35mpb.start[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Add unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor extend existing ExternalParser tests[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to cover:  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Rejection of commands containing invalid characters  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Successful launch of a harmless, whitelisted external parser when correctly[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfigured  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Fallback behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., skipping external parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when validation fails  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Verify no changes to harness or test code are required; all existing CI tests[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould pass unmodified.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By eliminating `[0m[1;35mRuntime.exec[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and ad-hoc splitting, we avoid shell [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterpretation and injection entirely.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whitelisting and filesystem checks ensure only legitimate, [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madministrator-approved binaries are ever invoked.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Moving the exiftool-path configuration out of untrusted metadata closes the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent-to‐code injection channel.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using `ProcessBuilder` with explicit argument lists is a best practice [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepeatedly established elsewhere in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., other modules invoking [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal tools[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Administrators who relied on in-content metadata to set exiftool paths may see[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir overrides ignored. Communicate the change in release notes and document the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproper configuration approach.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Strict validation may block nonstandard installations; provide clear error [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessages and documentation on how to correctly configure the external parser path. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No performance impact beyond a one-time validation check per external parse [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvocation.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. No Harness or Fuzzing Logic Changes[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Jazzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`HtmlParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and test code remain untouched.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing will now trigger safe-path errors rather than reach OS command [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution, effectively closing the vulnerability without altering the fuzzer entry [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoints.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to apply an undefined `environmentOverrides` variable.[0m                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The compilation errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`environmentOverrides` not found[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m stem from leftover [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences to an undefined variable after switching from `Runtime.exec` to [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ProcessBuilder`. Additionally, we need to complete the hardening work around [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand validation and eliminate any token-splitting behavior that could [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreintroduce shell interpolation.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. ExternalParser.java Fix Steps  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Remove the two lines that reference `environmentOverrides` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines where [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mpb.environment[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.putAll[0m[1;39m([0m[39menvironmentOverrides[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` appears[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to restore compile [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintegrity.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace the entire `try`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`catch` block that invokes `Runtime.exec` with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimpler `ProcessBuilder` invocation using only the validated `cmd` array.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Ensure the pre-existing validation logic remains:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `cmd[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` must be an absolute path, exist on disk, and be executable.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - No token may contain shell metacharacters [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`; & | \` > <`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Consolidate the validation and command execution into a contiguous code [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion with correct braces and imports.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Concretely, in `ExternalParser.java` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround the existing lines [0m[1;36m287[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Build our command[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       String[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m cmd = new String[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcommand.length[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mSystem.arraycopy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, cmd, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, command.length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validate executable path[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       File exeFile = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmd[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mexeFile.isAbsolute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || ![0m[1;35mexeFile.exists[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || ![0m[1;35mexeFile.canExecute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           throw new [0m[1;35mTikaException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"External parser executable not valid: "[0m[39m + [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcmd[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validate tokens for shell metacharacters[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString token : cmd[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtoken.matches[0m[1;39m([0m[32m".*[0m[32m[[0m[32m;&|`><[0m[32m][0m[32m.*"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               throw new [0m[1;35mTikaException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid characters in external command [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mtoken: "[0m[39m + token[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the old `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmd.length == [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m … [0m[1;35mRuntime.getRuntime[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.exec` block with:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       Process process;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           ProcessBuilder pb = new [0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmd[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           process = [0m[1;35mpb.start[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           throw new [0m[1;35mTikaException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to start external process"[0m[39m, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove any import or field related to `environmentOverrides`.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. HtmlHandler.java Confirmation  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing patch in `HtmlHandler.java` that disables metadata-based [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exiftool` configuration is sound. No further changes are needed there.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Functionality  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The command array passed in remains unchanged: callers still supply one or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmore tokens.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do **not** reintroduce automated splitting of a single combined string [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mavoiding potential command-injection attack vectors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We eliminate the undefined variable references, ensuring the module compiles [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand runs the same fuzzer harness without altering its behavior.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and Side-Effects  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By removing `environmentOverrides` and simplifying to a direct [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mProcessBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcmd[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.start[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, we restore compilability and remove dead code.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retaining strict validation on both the executable and arguments preserves [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefense-in-depth against attacker-supplied metacharacters.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, test code, or external dependencies are modified—fuzzer entry [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoints remain intact.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential side-effect: callers that expected environment overrides will no [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger have that facility. If required in the future, re-introduce via a documented[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msetEnvironmentOverrides[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMap<String,String>[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` API.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run `mvn test-compile` to confirm no compilation errors.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Execute the existing HTML parser fuzzers; they should no longer trigger [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer’s OS command injection sanitizer, nor fail to compile.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Manually test a known-good external parser invocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., with a valid [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`executable` path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure proper startup and exit code propagation.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo additional file retrieval is required—the changes lie entirely within [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ExternalParser.java` and build on the already accepted HtmlHandler adjustments.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
